    function onClick (e) {
      var eventTrigger = e.target.closest("[data-event]");
      if (eventTrigger) {
        var eventName = eventTrigger.getAttribute("data-event");
        var properties = eventTrigger.getAttribute("data-event-properties");
        properties = properties ? JSON.parse(properties) : {};
        window.analytics.track(eventName, properties);

        // End here if function keys used since this typically means opening the URL in a new tab
        if (e.metaKey || e.shiftKey || e.ctrlKey || e.altKey) return;

        var href = eventTrigger.getAttribute("href");
        if (!href) return;
        e.preventDefault();
        setTimeout(function () { window.location.href = href }, 300);
      }
    }
